set RLIMIT_AS: {e}\")\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Data loading + crisp gold  (reused verbatim from iter-2 for cache identity)\n# ===========================================================================\ndef verbalize(h: str, r: str, t: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"CLUTRR triple (h, r, t) means 'tail is head's relation' => '{t} is the {r} of {h}.'\"\"\"\n    return f\"{t} is the {r} of {h}.\"\n\n\ndef _doc_seed(doc_id: str, salt: int = 0) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Stable per-document seed (hashlib, NOT Python's randomized hash()) so extraction\n    shuffles, decoy fallbacks and swaps are reproducible across runs and doc subsets.\"\"\"\n    h = hashlib.sha256(f\"{doc_id}|{SEED}|{salt}\".encode()).hexdigest()\n    return int(h[:12], 16)\n\n\nRELATION_VOCAB = [\"aunt\", \"brother\", \"daughter\", \"daughter-in-law\", \"father\",\n                  \"father-in-law\", \"granddaughter\", \"grandfather\", \"grandmother\",\n                  \"grandson\", \"husband\", \"mother\", \"mother-in-law\", \"nephew\", \"niece\",\n                  \"sister\", \"son\", \"son-in-law\", \"uncle\", \"wife\"]\n\n\nclass Doc:\n    __slots__ = (\"doc_id\", \"text\", \"entities\", \"query\", \"k\", \"is_pilot\", \"fold\",\n                 \"gold_true\", \"gold_rel\", \"gold_pairs\", \"atomic_pairs\", \"multi_pairs\",\n                 \"atomic_facts\", \"multi_facts\")\n\n    def __init__(self, raw: dict):\n        inp = json.loads(raw[\"input\"])\n        out = json.loads(raw[\"output\"])\n        self.doc_id = inp[\"doc_id\"]\n        self.text = inp[\"document_text\"]\n        self.entities = [e[\"name\"] for e in inp[\"entities\"]]\n        self.query = inp.get(\"query\", {})\n        self.k = int(raw[\"metadata_chain_length_k\"])\n        self.is_pilot = bool(raw[\"metadata_is_pilot\"])\n        self.fold = raw[\"metadata_fold\"]\n        self.atomic_facts = [(f[\"head\"], f[\"relation\"], f[\"tail\"]) for f in out[\"atomic_facts\"]]\n        self.multi_facts = [(f[\"head\"], f[\"relation\"], f[\"tail\"]) for f in out[\"multi_hop_facts\"]]\n        self.gold_true = set(self.atomic_facts) | set(self.multi_facts)\n        self.gold_rel: dict[tuple[str, str], str] = {}\n        for (hh, rr, tt) in self.gold_true:\n            self.gold_rel[(hh, tt)] = rr\n        self.atomic_pairs = [(h, t) for (h, r, t) in self.atomic_facts]\n        self.multi_pairs = [(h, t) for (h, r, t) in self.multi_facts]\n        self.gold_pairs = set(self.gold_rel.keys())\n\n    def label(self, h: str, r: str, t: str) -> str:\n        if (h, r, t) in self.gold_true:\n            return TRUE\n        if (h, t) in self.gold_pairs and r != self.gold_rel[(h, t)]:\n            return FALSE\n        return UND\n\n\ndef load_docs(path: Path, n_docs: int | None = None, pilot_only: bool = False) -> list[Doc]:\n    raw = json.loads(path.read_text())\n    examples = raw[\"datasets\"][0][\"examples\"]\n    docs = [Doc(e) for e in examples]\n    if pilot_only:\n        docs = [d for d in docs if d.is_pilot]\n    if n_docs is not None:\n        docs = docs[:n_docs]\n    return docs\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Prompts  (reused verbatim from iter-2 EXP2 for self-consistency cache identity)\n# ===========================================================================\ndef extract_messages(doc: Doc, pairs: list[tuple[str, str]]) -> list[dict]:\n    vocab = \", \".join(RELATION_VOCAB)\n    stubs = \"\\n\".join(f\"{i+1}. {t} is the ___ of {h}\" for i, (h, t) in enumerate(pairs))\n    sysmsg = (\"You extract kinship facts from a short story. Use ONLY these relation \"\n              f\"words (exact spelling): {vocab}.\")\n    user = (f\"Document:\\n{doc.text}\\n\\n\"\n            f\"People: {', '.join(doc.entities)}\\n\\n\"\n            \"TASK 1 (STATED FACTS): List every kinship relationship DIRECTLY stated in the \"\n            \"text, each as one sentence of the form \\\"<Person> is the <relation> of <Person>\\\".\\n\\n\"\n            \"TASK 2 (INFERRED RELATIONS): Complete each numbered statement below with the \"\n            \"single most likely relation word from the vocabulary. The relationship may be \"\n            \"directly stated or require reasoning over the family tree. Give exactly one \"\n            \"relation per item, in order.\\n\"\n            f\"{stubs}\\n\\n\"\n            \"Respond with STRICT JSON only, no prose:\\n\"\n            \"{\\\"stated\\\": [\\\"<sentence>\\\", ...], \"\n            \"\\\"inferred\\\": [\\\"<relation_for_1>\\\", \\\"<relation_for_2>\\\", ...]}\")\n    return [{\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": sysmsg}, {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": user}]\n\n\ndef decoy_messages(doc: Doc, items: list[tuple[str, str, str]]) -> list[dict]:\n    vocab = \", \".join(RELATION_VOCAB)\n    lines = \"\\n\".join(f\"{i+1}. \\\"{t} is the {r} of {h}\\\"  (current relation: {r})\"\n                      for i, (h, r, t) in enumerate(items))\n    sysmsg = (\"You propose alternative kinship relations. Use ONLY these relation words \"\n              f\"(exact spelling): {vocab}.\")\n    user = (\"For each numbered statement below, give the TWO next most plausible \"\n            \"ALTERNATIVE relation words (each different from the current one), most \"\n            \"plausible first — a likely-but-possibly-wrong guess for that exact statement.\\n\"\n            f\"{lines}\\n\\n\"\n            \"Respond with STRICT JSON only: a JSON array with one [alt1, alt2] pair per \"\n            \"numbered item, in order: [[\\\"alt1\\\",\\\"alt2\\\"], [\\\"alt1\\\",\\\"alt2\\\"], ...]\")\n    return [{\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": sysmsg}, {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": user}]\n\n\ndef score_messages_portable(doc_text: str, claim: str) -> list[dict]:\n    return [\n        {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\":\n            \"You check whether a kinship claim is logically entailed by the document. \"\n            \"A claim is entailed if it is directly stated OR can be derived from stated facts.\"},\n        {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\":\n            f\"Document: {doc_text}\\n\\nClaim: {claim}\\n\"\n            \"Is this claim entailed by the document? Respond in EXACTLY this format:\\n\"\n            \"Answer: <Yes or No>\\nConfidence: <integer 0-100>\"},\n    ]\n\n\nSCORE_VB_SYS = (\"You assess whether a kinship claim is entailed by a short document. \"\n                \"A claim is entailed if it is directly stated OR can be derived from \"\n                \"stated facts.\")\n\n\ndef score_messages_verbalized(doc_text: str, claim: str) -> list[dict]:\n    \"\"\"Single-call verbalized confidence (0-100). The documented discreteness/loose-target\n    contrast elicitation (iter-2 showed verbalized tail win-rate anti-conservative).\"\"\"\n    return [\n        {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": SCORE_VB_SYS},\n        {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\":\n            f\"Document: {doc_text}\\n\\nClaim: {claim}\\n\"\n            \"Give ONLY an integer 0-100 = your confidence (percent) that the claim is \"\n            \"true/entailed by the document. No words, just the number.\"},\n    ]\n\n\n_STATED_RE = None\n\n\ndef parse_stated_sentences(text: str) -> set:\n    import re\n    global _STATED_RE\n    if _STATED_RE is None:\n        _STATED_RE = re.compile(r\"([A-Z][a-zA-Z]+)\\s+is\\s+the\\s+([a-zA-Z\\-]+)\\s+of\\s+([A-Z][a-zA-Z]+)\")\n    out = set()\n    for m in _STATED_RE.finditer(text or \"\"):\n        b, r, a = m.group(1), _norm_rel(m.group(2)), m.group(3)\n        if r:\n            out.add((a, r, b))\n    return out\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# JSON parsing from LLM output\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\ndef _extract_json(text: str | None):\n    if not text:\n        return None\n    t = text.strip()\n    if t.startswith(\"```\"):\n        t = t.strip(\"`\")\n        if t[:4].lower() == \"json\":\n            t = t[4:]\n    for opener, closer in ((\"{\", \"}\"), (\"[\", \"]\")):\n        i = t.find(opener)\n        if i == -1:\n            continue\n        depth = 0\n        for j in range(i, len(t)):\n            if t[j] == opener:\n                depth += 1\n            elif t[j] == closer:\n                depth -= 1\n                if depth == 0:\n                    try:\n                        return json.loads(t[i:j + 1])\n                    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                        break\n    try:\n        return json.loads(t)\n    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n        return None\n\n\ndef _norm_rel(r) -> str | None:\n    if not isinstance(r, str):\n        return None\n    r = r.strip().lower()\n    return r if r in RELATION_VOCAB else None\n\n\ndef _parse_prob(text: str | None) -> float | None:\n    if not text:\n        return None\n    import re\n    m = re.search(r\"[-+]?\\d*\\.?\\d+\", text)\n    if not m:\n        return None\n    try:\n        v = float(m.group(0))\n    except ValueError:\n        return None\n    if v > 1.0:\n        v = v / 100.0\n    return float(min(1.0, max(0.0, v)))\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Extraction (one call/doc) -> reals (labeled) + atomic P/R + multi-hop accuracy\n#   reused verbatim from iter-2 EXP2 so the extraction call hits the warm cache\n# ===========================================================================\nasync def extract_doc(client: OpenRouterClient, doc: Doc, rng: random.Random) -> dict:\n    pairs = list(doc.atomic_pairs) + list(doc.multi_pairs)\n    pair_type = {p: \"atomic\" for p in doc.atomic_pairs}\n    for p in doc.multi_pairs:\n        pair_type.setdefault(p, \"multi_hop\")\n    shuffled = pairs[:]\n    rng.shuffle(shuffled)\n    res = await client.call(PRIMARY_MODEL, extract_messages(doc, shuffled),\n                            max_tokens=900, temperature=0.0)\n    parsed = _extract_json(res[\"content\"]) or {}\n    stated = parsed.get(\"stated\") if isinstance(parsed, dict) else None\n    inferred = parsed.get(\"inferred\") if isinstance(parsed, dict) else None\n    stated = stated if isinstance(stated, list) else []\n    inferred = inferred if isinstance(inferred, list) else []\n\n    stated_triples = set()\n    stated_text_parts = []\n    for s in stated:\n        if isinstance(s, str):\n            stated_text_parts.append(s)\n        elif isinstance(s, list) and len(s) == 3:\n            h, r, t = str(s[0]).strip(), _norm_rel(s[1]), str(s[2]).strip()\n            if r:\n                stated_triples.add((h, r, t))\n    for (a, r, b) in parse_stated_sentences(\"\\n\".join(stated_text_parts)):\n        if a in doc.entities and b in doc.entities:\n            stated_triples.add((a, r, b))\n    gold_atomic = set(doc.atomic_facts)\n    tp = len(stated_triples & gold_atomic)\n    prec = tp / len(stated_triples) if stated_triples else float(\"nan\")\n    rec = tp / len(gold_atomic) if gold_atomic else float(\"nan\")\n\n    pred_rel: dict[tuple[str, str], str] = {}\n    for idx, (h, t) in enumerate(shuffled):\n        r = _norm_rel(inferred[idx]) if idx < len(inferred) else None\n        if r:\n            pred_rel[(h, t)] = r\n    reals = []\n    n_mh_correct = n_mh_total = 0\n    for (h, t) in pairs:\n        r = pred_rel.get((h, t))\n        if r is None:\n            continue\n        lab = doc.label(h, r, t)\n        ftype = pair_type[(h, t)]\n        if ftype == \"multi_hop\":\n            n_mh_total += 1\n            if r == doc.gold_rel.get((h, t)):\n                n_mh_correct += 1\n        reals.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:real:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                      \"h\": h, \"r\": r, \"t\": t, \"fact_type\": ftype, \"label\": lab,\n                      \"claim\": verbalize(h, r, t)})\n    return {\"doc_id\": doc.doc_id, \"reals\": reals, \"atomic_prec\": prec, \"atomic_rec\": rec,\n            \"n_stated\": len(stated_triples), \"n_pairs\": len(pairs),\n            \"mh_acc\": (n_mh_correct / n_mh_total) if n_mh_total else float(\"nan\"),\n            \"n_mh\": n_mh_total}\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Decoy / ladder-rung / entrapment construction\n# ===========================================================================\ndef verify_nonentailed(doc: Doc, h: str, r: str, t: str, avoid: set) -> bool:\n    if r in avoid:\n        return False\n    if (h, r, t) in doc.gold_true:\n        return False\n    if (h, t) in doc.gold_pairs and r == doc.gold_rel[(h, t)]:\n        return False\n    return True\n\n\nasync def gen_counterfactual_decoys(client: OpenRouterClient, doc: Doc, reals: list[dict],\n                                    model: str, rng: random.Random):\n    \"\"\"Return (decoys_L4, decoys2_L3, n_generated, n_contaminated). ONE batched call/doc\n    (cache-identical to iter-2 for cf=L4). cf2=L3 = the second verified-non-entailed\n    alternative parsed from the SAME (already-cached) generation, so it costs no new gen.\"\"\"\n    items = [(c[\"h\"], c[\"r\"], c[\"t\"]) for c in reals]\n    if not items:\n        return [], [], 0, 0\n    res = await client.call(model, decoy_messages(doc, items), max_tokens=700, temperature=0.0)\n    parsed = _extract_json(res[\"content\"])\n    decoys, decoys2, n_gen, n_contam = [], [], 0, 0\n    for i, c in enumerate(reals):\n        h, t, r_real = c[\"h\"], c[\"t\"], c[\"r\"]\n        gold_r = doc.gold_rel.get((h, t))\n        if isinstance(parsed, list):\n            alts = parsed[i] if i < len(parsed) else None\n        elif isinstance(parsed, dict):\n            alts = parsed.get(str(i + 1))\n        else:\n            alts = None\n        cand_rels = []\n        if isinstance(alts, list):\n            for a in alts:\n                rr = _norm_rel(a)\n                if rr:\n                    n_gen += 1\n                    if rr == gold_r:\n                        n_contam += 1\n                    cand_rels.append(rr)\n        avoid = {r_real}\n        chosen = []                       # collect up to 2 distinct verified-non-entailed alts\n        for rr in cand_rels:\n            if rr not in chosen and verify_nonentailed(doc, h, rr, t, avoid):\n                chosen.append(rr)\n            if len(chosen) >= 2:\n                break\n        # deterministic fallback to fill the 1st (cf) slot exactly as iter-2 did\n        if not chosen:\n            pool = [x for x in RELATION_VOCAB if verify_nonentailed(doc, h, x, t, avoid)]\n            if pool:\n                chosen.append(pool[rng.randrange(len(pool))])\n        if not chosen:\n            continue\n        decoys.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:cf:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                       \"h\": h, \"r\": chosen[0], \"t\": t, \"pair\": (h, t),\n                       \"real_id\": c[\"cand_id\"], \"claim\": verbalize(h, chosen[0], t)})\n        # cf2 (L3): a SECOND distinct alternative; deterministic fallback if only one alt\n        r2 = chosen[1] if len(chosen) >= 2 else None\n        if r2 is None:\n            pool = [x for x in RELATION_VOCAB\n                    if x != chosen[0] and verify_nonentailed(doc, h, x, t, avoid)]\n            if pool:\n                r2 = pool[rng.randrange(len(pool))]\n        if r2 is not None:\n            decoys2.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:cf2:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                            \"h\": h, \"r\": r2, \"t\": t, \"real_id\": c[\"cand_id\"],\n                            \"claim\": verbalize(h, r2, t)})\n    return decoys, decoys2, n_gen, n_contam\n\n\ndef gen_swaps(doc: Doc, reals: list[dict], rng: random.Random) -> list[dict]:\n    \"\"\"L1 random in-document swap: tail -> another in-doc entity (kept relation).\"\"\"\n    swaps = []\n    persons = list(doc.entities)\n    for c in reals:\n        h, r, t = c[\"h\"], c[\"r\"], c[\"t\"]\n        pool = [p for p in persons if p != t and p != h\n                and verify_nonentailed(doc, h, r, p, set())]\n        if not pool:\n            continue\n        tp = pool[rng.randrange(len(pool))]\n        swaps.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:swap:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                      \"h\": h, \"r\": r, \"t\": tp, \"real_id\": c[\"cand_id\"],\n                      \"claim\": verbalize(h, r, tp)})\n    return swaps\n\n\ndef gen_random_vocab(doc: Doc, reals: list[dict], rng: random.Random) -> list[dict]:\n    \"\"\"L2 random-vocab: keep the entities, swap the relation to a random non-entailed\n    vocabulary relation (medium difficulty).\"\"\"\n    out = []\n    for c in reals:\n        h, r, t = c[\"h\"], c[\"r\"], c[\"t\"]\n        pool = [x for x in RELATION_VOCAB if verify_nonentailed(doc, h, x, t, {r})]\n        if not pool:\n            continue\n        rr = pool[rng.randrange(len(pool))]\n        out.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:rv:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                    \"h\": h, \"r\": rr, \"t\": t, \"real_id\": c[\"cand_id\"],\n                    \"claim\": verbalize(h, rr, t)})\n    return out\n\n\ndef gen_foreign_swap(doc: Doc, reals: list[dict], foreign_names: list[str],\n                     rng: random.Random, salt_tag: str, cid_tag: str) -> list[dict]:\n    \"\"\"L0 foreign-swap / entrapment: tail -> an entity sampled from a DIFFERENT document\n    (out-of-context, false-by-construction; relation kept). Deterministic per (doc, real).\n    Used for L0 (cid_tag='fgn') and, with an independent draw, for ENTRAPMENT (cid_tag='ent').\"\"\"\n    out = []\n    in_doc = set(doc.entities)\n    for c in reals:\n        h, r, t = c[\"h\"], c[\"r\"], c[\"t\"]\n        # deterministic per-(doc,real,salt) seed via hashlib (NEVER python hash()): stable\n        # foreign-entity draws across processes/runs so cache keys are reproducible.\n        sd = int(hashlib.sha256(f\"{doc.doc_id}|{h}|{t}|{salt_tag}|{SEED}\".encode()).hexdigest()[:12], 16)\n        rloc = random.Random(sd)\n        # pick a foreign name not in this document (guaranteed non-entailed)\n        cand = None\n        for _ in range(8):\n            nm = foreign_names[rloc.randrange(len(foreign_names))]\n            if nm not in in_doc and nm != h:\n                cand = nm\n                break\n        if cand is None:\n            continue\n        out.append({\"cand_id\": f\"{doc.doc_id}:{cid_tag}:{h}>{t}\", \"doc_id\": doc.doc_id,\n                    \"h\": h, \"r\": r, \"t\": cand, \"real_id\": c[\"cand_id\"],\n                    \"claim\": verbalize(h, r, cand)})\n    return out\n\n\n_SALTS = {\"extract\": 0, \"decoy\": 7, \"swap\": 99, \"rv\": 13, \"fgn\": 23, \"ent\": 41}\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Scoring (isolated, provenance-blinded). sc => K_SC calls; vb => 1 call.\n# ===========================================================================\nasync def score_portable(client: OpenRouterClient, model: str, doc_text: str, claim: str) -> float:\n    \"\"\"K=5 self-consistency (headline). Cache-identical to iter-2 EXP2.score_portable.\"\"\"\n    ps = []\n    for i in range(K_SC):\n        from llm_client import parse_yes_conf\n        res = await client.call(model, score_messages_portable(doc_text, claim),\n                                max_tokens=24, temperature=0.7, seed=SEED + i, sample_idx=i)\n        p = parse_yes_conf(res[\"content\"])\n        if p is not None:\n            ps.append(p)\n    return float(np.mean(ps)) if ps else 0.5\n\n\nasync def score_verbalized(client: OpenRouterClient, model: str, doc_text: str, claim: str) -> float:\n    res = ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nasync def run_batched(coros: list, batch: int, label: str, client: OpenRouterClient):\n    out = []\n    for i in range(0, Used inside the doc-block bootstrap hot loop so the powered (B>=2000) diagonal\n# over ~thousands of reals finishes in seconds rather than O(distinct|W|^2) minutes.\ndef _knockoff_fast(W: np.ndarray, alpha: float):\n    Wa = np.asarray(W, dtype=float)\n    if Wa.size == 0:\n        return math.inf, 0, 1.0\n    sW = np.sort(Wa)\n    mags = np.unique(np.abs(Wa))\n    mags = mags[mags > 0.0]\n    if For each bin compute the\\n#     PAIRED per-pair sign-flip win-rate + realized FDR at the cutoff + doc-block CI. metadata.density_strata.\\n#     If the paired failure PERSISTS across bins (esp. holds at LOW density) -> the failure is NOT merely\\n#     error-density-driven. If it VANISHES at LOW density -> scope the limitation to the error-dense regime.\\n# (b) BUDGET-GATED STRONGER-EXTRACTOR arm (the decisive de-confound; run only if cost < $3 after Phase 5):\\n#     Re-run EXTRACTION with STRONG_EXTRACTOR (gpt-4.1-mini) over the multi_hop family on the full corpus if\\n#     affordable, else a powered subset (>=150 docs). KEEP the SCORER fixed at nano-SC (isolates the EXTRACTOR\\n#     effect). Generate cf decoys for the new reals; score reals+decoys (nano-SC). Recompute, for this stronger\\n#     extractor: multi_hop accuracy (expect lift from ~0.17), realized FDR vs alpha diagonal, decoy_fdr_hat,\\n#     and the PAIRED win-rate at the cutoff. metadata.strong_extractor_arm = {extractor, n_docs, mh_acc,\\n#     diagonal_rows, paired_win_rate, realized_fdr_at_alpha_star, verdict}.\\n#     VERDICT logic (pre-registered): if paired sign-flip failure PERSISTS with the competent extractor ->\\n#     'marginal != paired is a property of the LLM boundary' is EARNED (headline). If it VANISHES (gate now\\n#     controls realized FDR <= alpha) -> report the POSITIVE result 'the gate controls FDR when the extractor\\n#     can score its own errors' and SCOPE the limitation to the weak-scorer/error-dense regime. Either outcome\\n#     is publishable; record which fired.\\n\\n# ========================= PHASE 7 (NEW #3)  S1b LADDER: power-or-bound =========================\\nladder = analyze_s1b_ladder(pipe) over LADDER=[L0_foreign_swap(fgn), L1_random_swap(swap), L2_random_vocab(rv),\\n    L3_cf_2nd(cf2), L4_cf_1st(cf)] scored under the SAME K=5 self-consistency.\\nPOWER it: score the rungs on the (enlarged ~122-doc) pilot UNION the first ~100 confirmatory docs until EACH\\n    rung has >= N_LADDER_FALSE_MIN=30 FALSE pairs (record realized n per rung). For each rung report tail\\n    win-rate over false pairs + KS/MW + doc-block CI + detected_anti_conservative flag.\\nIf a rung cannot reach the floor within budget -> report it PURELY as 'underpowered; cannot localize which decoy\\n    classes are detected; cannot certify paired validity' and DELETE the contradicted 'detects only gross decoys'\\n    narrative (iter-3 data showed L0 foreign-swap detected=FALSE while L1-L4 in-distribution=TRUE, the opposite).\\n\\n# ========================= PHASE 8  ENTRAPMENT + DISCONFIRMATION + BH + FIGURES + OUTPUT =========================\\nfor family,alpha in [(disconf_family, alpha_star), (disconf_family, 0.50)]:\\n    entrap[family,alpha] = entrapment_analysis(pipe, family, alpha)   # Wen 2025 combined bound\\n        FDP_hat = N_E*(1+1/r)/(N_T+N_E), r=1 (paired) at alpha* AND 0.50; report agreement with realized + decoy.\\nverdict = primary_disconfirmation(pipe, norm_sc, diag['multi_hop'])  # DISCONFIRMED iff realized FDR exceeds\\n    operative alpha by > TAU AND the doc-block-bootstrap CI lies entirely on the anti-conservative side, under\\n    isolated self-consistency at adequate power; self-report additionally disconfirmed if decoy_fdr_hat anti-conservative.\\nbh = collect_bh(diag_sc, ladder, crux_sc, crux_vb, entrap)            # BH q=0.05 across ALL validation tests.\\nFIGURES (make_figures, extend captions to be FULL & self-contained):\\n    F1 per-family realized-FDR-vs-alpha DIAGONAL: method(cf) vs PLAIN-threshold vs SWAP, with doc-block CI bands,\\n       the 1/k minimum-estimable-FDR floor drawn, decoy_fdr_hat overlaid per alpha, certified cells marked.\\n    F2 CRUX overlaid CDFs (decoy / spontaneous-error / true-positive) with the PAIRED-win asymmetry annotated and\\n       the four-test (KS/MW/AD/perm) p-values in the caption (marginal-holds-while-paired-fails annotated).\\n    F3 PAIRED win-rate across the 4 (G,S) configs with CIs and the 0.5 line.\\n    F4 DE-CONFOUND: paired win-rate / realized FDR vs false-positive-density bins (+ stronger-extractor point).\\n    F5 S1b ladder L0..L4 win-rate + CIs with the per-rung false-pair n in the caption.\\n    Every caption states: 1/k floor, B=2000 doc-block bootstrap, the n it rests on, and the verdict it supports.\\nbuild_output(pipe, analysis, out_path='method_out.json')  # schema exp_gen_sol_out: metadata{ all diagonals,\\n    power/populability table, triple per cell, self-report flags, marginal crux, PAIRED block + paired_across_GS,\\n    density_strata, strong_extractor_arm, S1b verdict, entrapment, BH table, primary-disconfirmation verdict,\\n    runtime+cost, full figure captions } + per-real examples (SC/VB Z, W, per-alpha admission predictions).\\nVALIDATE with aii-json skill against exp_gen_sol_out; if >100MB use aii-file-size-limit to split. Write README.\\nFINAL cost report from logs/cost.jsonl; assert < $10; figures/ populated; selftest still green.\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"BUDGET (primary risk). The full over-generation SC scoring of ~593 docs minus the warm-cached 190-prefix is the main cost. Mitigations in priority order, each triggered when logs/cost.jsonl crosses SOFT_CAP_USD=$4: (1) drop N_EXTRACT_SAMPLES from 2 to 1 (legacy T=0.0 cache-identical extraction) — removes the live over-gen scoring; (2) cap the corpus at the largest n already scored (e.g. --n-docs 300) and report the realized n honestly as the power achieved — even ~300 docs gives >>40 genuine false reals, far above the 12-pair tail; (3) restrict the STRONGER-EXTRACTOR de-confound arm to a 150-doc powered subset, then to pilot-only, then SKIP it (the FREE k-density stratification still de-confounds error-density vs intrinsic-failure with zero API); (4) restrict the (G,S) paired analysis to the cached 190-prefix only (warm, ~$0) and mark wider configs underpowered; (5) restrict ladder/verbalized/entrapment to the pilot slice via the existing --light flag. Do NOT relax the canonical simple-path crisp-gold constraint (that would poison the realized-FDR ground truth).\\n\\nDE-CONFOUND VANISHES vs PERSISTS — both are planned outcomes, not failures: if the paired sign-flip failure VANISHES with the stronger extractor or at LOW false-positive density, report the POSITIVE 'gate controls realized FDR at alpha when the extractor can score its own errors' and SCOPE the limitation to the weak-scorer/error-dense regime; if it PERSISTS across extractor strength and density, the 'marginal != paired at the LLM boundary' headline is earned. Else SOFTEN the claim to 'only marginal robustness to G!=S\\n        is demonstrated' (per S2b mandate). Carry the MARGINAL G!=S result forward as SETTLED (no new budget).\\n\\n# ========================= PHASE 6 (NEW #2)  DE-CONFOUND extractor strength / false-positive density =========================\\n# Goal: distinguish 'knockoffs fundamentally do not transfer at the LLM boundary' (intrinsic) from\\n# 'this single weak-extractor, error-dense regime is too noisy' (confound = nano multi_hop acc ~0.17, ~85% false).\\n# (a) FREE density stratification (zero extra API): bin multi_hop FALSE pairs by chain length k into\\n#     LOW (k in 2-3), MED (k in 4-6), HIGH (k in 7-10) -> a natural genuine-false-density gradient\\n#     (~20% / ~50% / ~85% false among admitted reals, verified empirically per bin). For each bin compute the\\n#     PAIRED per-pair sign-flip win-rate + realized FDR at the cutoff + doc-block CI. metadata.density_strata.\\n#     If the paired failure PERSISTS across bins (esp. holds at LOW density) -> the failure is NOT merely\\n#     error-density-driven. If it VANISHES at LOW density -> scope the limitation to the error-dense regime.\\n# (b) BUDGET-GATED STRONGER-EXTRACTOR arm (the decisive de-confound; run only if cost < $3 after Phase 5):\\n#     Re-run EXTRACTION with STRONG_EXTRACTOR (gpt-4.1-mini) over the multi_hop family on the full corpus if\\n#     affordable, else a powered subset (>=150 docs). Do NOT relax the canonical simple-path crisp-gold constraint (that would poison the realized-FDR ground truth).\\n\\nDE-CONFOUND VANISHES vs PERSISTS — both are planned outcomes, not failures: if the paired sign-flip failure VANISHES with the stronger extractor or at LOW false-positive density, report the POSITIVE 'gate controls realized FDR at alpha when the extractor can score its own errors' and SCOPE the limitation to the weak-scorer/error-dense regime; if it PERSISTS across extractor strength and density, the 'marginal != paired at the LLM boundary' headline is earned. The S1b rung that cannot reach 30 false pairs is reported purely as 'underpowered; cannot certify paired validity' with the contradicted 'gross-decoy' narrative deleted.\\n\\nCROSS-FAMILY MINISTRAL SCORES MISSING. ## What I delivered

A detailed, executor-ready EXPERIMENT plan for **iter-4 P1 — the headline "power & de-confound the self-consistency CLUTRR FDR calibration diagonal"** artifact. The key insight that shaped it: iter-3's P1 code (`art_sBLQqsdm3EIA`) was already *designed* for ~593 docs but was only *executed* on a 40-doc checkpoint, so iter-4's job is to **power and extend ~95%-existing tested code**, not rebuild.

**The three real additions the plan specifies (everything else is reuse):**
1. **POWER** — regenerate the corpus to ~593 docs (concrete scaled `CONFIRM_COUNTS` with k≥6 oversampling), enlarge the pilot to power the S1b ladder, add T=0.7 over-generation extraction, run the full per-family diagonal with the `(alpha, decoy_fdr_hat, realized FDR)` triple + doc-block bootstrap CIs + self-report disconfirmation, so crux p-values move off the ~0.06 borderline.
2. **NEW paired-exchangeability statistic** reported distinctly from the marginal win-rate **and computed across the four (Generator, Scorer) configs** (incl. cross-family ministral-8b), mostly on the warm-cached 190-doc prefix (~$0) — evidencing paired-layer de-circularization.
3. **DE-CONFOUND** — a free k-density stratification (LOW/MED/HIGH false-density bins) as P1's self-contained de-confound, plus a budget-gated stronger-extractor preview.

**Concrete executor guidance throughout:** exact reusable function names (`diagonal_for_family`, `analyze_crux`, `analyze_s1b_ladder`, `knockoff_plus_threshold`, `OpenRouterClient`…), the warm-cache prefix-superset trick (only new docs cost money), gradual-scaling checkpoints with a determinism/cache sanity gate, background+PID execution (avoiding the iter-2 block-polling crash), `cpu_heavy` profile, soft cap $4 / hard stop $10, full figure-caption requirements, and schema validation.

I also reconciled scope against the **sibling iter-4 artifacts** surfaced in MEMORY: the application anchor (P2/dir-app), the ProbLog reasoner (P4/dir4), and the dedicated extractor-strength × density de-confound matrix (dir2) are each owned elsewhere — so the plan stays focused on P1 and explicitly delegates the full de-confound matrix to dir2 to prevent duplicate spend. Recorded the plan and these decisions in memory.
